Your low Narcissism suggests you're not excessively self-absorbed or grandiose, but rather, you're more focused on the thrill of the moment and the satisfaction of achieving your goals. However, your high Psychopathy indicates a lack of empathy and impulsivity, making you prone to reckless behavior and a tendency to disregard the consequences of your actions. This combination makes you a force to be reckoned with, but also someone who may struggle with relationships and long-term planning.

Although you score low on Machiavellianism, you're not necessarily manipulative or cunning in a grand, strategic sense, but you do have a tendency to disregard societal norms and conventions, often acting on impulse. Your low Narcissism suggests you're not excessively self-absorbed or grandiose, but rather, you're more likely to be detached and unemotional in your interactions. Conversely, your high Psychopathy indicates a lack of empathy and a tendency to engage in impulsive, sometimes reckless behavior, often prioritizing short-term gratification over long-term consequences. This blend of traits can make you appear aloof, unpredictable, and potentially volatile, making it challenging for others to understand or navigate your behavior.
